# Weird JS Encoder

Static Site to transform JS code into valid letterless JS code

Site: [WeirdJSEncoder](https://heribertogm.github.io/WeirdJSEncoder/)

Example:
Input:
`console.log("Hello World!");`
Output:
`eval(([]+[])[({}+[])[+!![] + +!![] + +!![] + +!![] + +!![]]+({}+[])[+!![]]+((+!![]/+[])+[])[+!![] + +!![] + +!![] + +!![]]+(![]+[])[+!![] + +!![] + +!![]]+({}+[])[+!![] + +!![] + +!![] + +!![] +
